<userid>114642244097172381651< /userid><user_name>Daniel Cases< /user_name>< Date>

<rate>5</rate>< Review>
I was referred to Dr. Winter from my wife after I had sustained a chipped tooth. I was told that she was great with cosmetic dentistry and that her and her entire office staff was extremely friendly. My experience was just that and more! Upon entering, Alicia and Deb at the front desk were super friendly and helpful which is huge to me since dentist visits are not generally my most exciting appointments. I was then escorted back by Kat whom I believe was the dental assistant and she too was very friendly and gave me a tour of the office and introduced me to most of the other staff members that we passed by. Once taken to my chair, Kat helped answer all of my questions and helped me understand what we were doing that day and what to expect. When Dr. Winter came in, she was also very nice and friendly like no other dentist I've gone to. As her and Kat were doing their work, they checked in with me periodically to make sure I was doing fine and I don't think I had ever felt so relaxed during dental work! I almost felt as though I could have dozed off in a good, relaxing way. I was impressed at how well my tooth looked after the appointment and started discussing other dental plans I had considered. After the initial visit, I scheduled my next visit and plan to be a long time patient from here forward! I would definitely advise looking into visiting her practice if you are in the market for a home-base dental office or are just tired of feeling anxious about your current appointments! You won't be disappointment by Dr. Winter and her lovely staff!<//Review>

< review>
FOOD pizza was good. Favorite was pesto where you add toppings. We added pepperoni, sausage, and bell peppers. Bell peppers are sliced thin which is nice. Crust was good and soft. Pastrami pizza pie was good too, more savory. Their ranch dipping sauce is really good. I'm not sure if they make it in house or if they order it from somewhere it sure is good. Three sizes of pizza.

INSIDE casual feel. Definitely sell beer here. Tv 's begins the counter and in the middle. Some arcade games in the other room. Staff was attentive, chill, and straight forward.

PARKING outside lot shared with other businesses in the small plaza. Look for the pizza and pasta sign.< /review>

< Text>
Really, really great. The poutine is fantastic. Good portion sizes. A petit is enough for a full meal. Meal is for 2-3 people. Burgers aren't AMAZING, but they're pretty good. Lots of toppings to choose from, and they're pretty generous with them. You absolutely have to try the authentic if you've never had poutine before. Once you're used to that, the Mexican Fiesta, Rocky, and the pulled pork one are all really good. Go stop by and try something. You won't regret it.</Text>

<rating>5</rating>< Text>
We live about 25 miles away, but often make the trek to eat here. There are a lot of other places that make something they claim is "Poutine", but somehow they screw up the gravy or cheese.  Not here. The Authentic is the best poutine I've had outside of Quebec! Crispy fries, squeaky cheddar cheese curds, amazing Brown gravy. Mmmmm.

The Spuddburger is basically an Authentic on a burger... possibly the best of both Canadian and American comfort food.  So good!

The staff and owner are friendly and helpful. Spudds is definitely recommended, especially if you're a Canadian expat looking for a real taste of home.</Text>

<rating>5<//rating>< text>
Been here twice and will definitely come again, great burgers.  Their pretzel bun is a great compliment to a great burger.  I went simple cheese 2/3 lb patty and regular fixin's.  BUT this is not to convince you of what this place is really about...poutine!  The pulled pork poutine is to die for.  If you want a simple plain ol' Poutine you'll be pleasantly surprised.  Good curd and good gravy and tons of options to please all the foodies out there.  Come give it a try you won't be disappointed.</text>

<user_id>102256588997957643557< /user_id><Rating>4<//Rating>< Text>
San Pedro is starting to grow on me with another hidden gem! I've heard that there are many great breakfast/brunch places in San Pedro and this is one of them.

My friend and I arrived here on a Saturday morning around 11am. Since we opted for first available seating, we were led outside to their small patio. The waitress took our order and the food arrived shortly after.

I had the veggie scramble with breakfast potatoes and a lemon muffin. I pretty much licked my plate clean and did NOT feel uncomfortably full. The veggie scramble was made with fresh veggies such as mushrooms, mini broccoli, tomatoes, onions, and zucchini. Everything tasted "light" and not much grease was left on the plate. The potatoes were seasoned and cooked just right.

I had a couple of bites of the lemon muffin and I really enjoyed the small lemon chunks, it made the muffin unique in texture as well as taste. It wasn't too sweet or dense.

Service was friendly and efficient. Portions are fair. Credit cards are accepted. What more can I ask for?!

By the way, street parking only, but not too difficult.< /Text>

<Date>1542898858538< /Date>< user_name>
Erica Chuvichien< /user_name>
<pictures>None< /pictures>< text>
BLACK FRIDAY REVIEW ONLY-

I am a normal KOHLS shopper. I typically shop the clearance racks and try to use coupons or KOHLS cash to make my savings go further.

However, for Black Friday, the KOHLS cash you get beforehand is not applicable to be used on black Friday. It starts on the 24th, that Saturday. Because of this you dont get the best savings or deals. For example, on black Friday the xbox 360 S with 1T is selling at Wal-Mart for $199, Target for $199 plus a $10 Target gift card.....but Kohls is selling it for $299 and $60 kohls cash. So even with the given kohls cash you're still overpaying by $40. There are many examples like this throughout Black Fridays sale at Kohls. Majority of their items are severely overpriced and they do not price match. However, buying their higher sale priced items stacked with your 20% or 30% coupons really makes the difference. Kohls controls the 15%, 20%, 25% offs. The manufacturers controls their 30%, 40%, 50% or higher sales. So this is where your Kohls coupons really pushes your savings!! They will be selling a serta cool gel topper for 50% off...and coupons are avail on it. This item is normally $250, but after all the coupons and savings you can get it for $89 for the queen! That's the cheapest price anywhere! You just have to do your homework!!

I've done Black Friday since every year since 1995 and I'd advise to look at Wal-Mart or even Target for the exact items first. Now, dont get me wrong, I love Kohls, but if you're looking for something specific and a great deal than search for it first.

Amazon, Groupon, Kohls, and Target shopping at most of these places a day beforehand might actually be cheaper than getting it on  "Black friday" itself. I bought what we wanted to buy on Black Friday at Kohls 2 days before Black Friday and used my Kohls cash and coupons and what wouldve been a $300 purchase for only $40.

Kohls employees are always super helpful and sometimes they help you out if you forget your ad coupons at home!! Dont be rude since many of these young kids are seasonal during this time of year!

Happy thanksgiving and happy hunting!!< /text>
